\tmark_pages_wc(chip, &chip->rb, true);\n727: \treturn 0;\n728: }\n729: \n730: static void azx_init_cmd_io(struct azx *chip)\n731: {\n732: \tspin_lock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n733: \t/* CORB set up */\n734: \tchip->corb.addr = chip->rb.addr;\n735: \tchip->corb.buf = (u32 *)chip->rb.area;\n736: \tazx_writel(chip, CORBLBASE, (u32)chip->corb.addr);\n737: \tazx_writel(chip, CORBUBASE, */\n742: \tazx_writew(chip, CORBWP, 0);\n743: \t/* reset the corb hw read pointer */\n744: \tazx_writew(chip, CORBRP, ICH6_CORBRP_RST);\n745: \t/* enable corb dma */\n746: \tazx_writeb(chip, CORBCTL, ICH6_CORBCTL_RUN);\n747: \n748: \t/* RIRB set up */\n749: \tchip->rirb.addr = chip->rb.addr + 2048;\n750: \tchip->rirb.buf = (u32 *)(chip->rb.area + 2048);\n751: \tchip->rirb.wp = chip->rirb.rp = \n756: \t/* set the rirb size to 256 entries (ULI requires explicitly) */\n757: \tazx_writeb(chip, RIRBSIZE, 0x02);\n758: \t/* reset the rirb hw write pointer */\n759: \tazx_writew(chip, RIRBWP, ICH6_RIRBWP_RST);\n760: \t/* set N=1, get RIRB response interrupt for new entry */\n761: \tif (chip->driver_caps & AZX_DCAPS_CTX_WORKAROUND)\n762: \t\tazx_writew(chip, RINTCNT, 0xc0);\n763: \telse\n764: \t\tazx_writew(chip, RINTCNT, 1);\n765: \t/* enable rirb dma and response irq */\n766: \tazx_writeb(chip, RIRBCTL, ICH6_RBCTL_DMA_EN | ICH6_RBCTL_IRQ_EN);\n767: \tspin_unlock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n768: }\n769: \n770: static void azx_free_cmd_io(struct azx *chip)\n771: {\n772: \tspin_lock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n773: \t/* disable ringbuffer DMAs */\n774: \tazx_writeb(chip, RIRBCTL, 0);\n775: \tazx_writeb(chip, CORBCTL, 0);\n776: \tspin_unlock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n777: }\n778: \n779: static unsigned int azx_command_addr(u32 cmd)\n780: {\n781: \tunsigned int addr = cmd >> 28;\n782: \n783: \tif (addr >= AZX_MAX_CODECS) {\n784: \t\tsnd_BUG();\n785: \t\taddr = 0;\n786: \t}\n787: \n788: \treturn addr;\n789: }\n790: \n791: static unsigned int azx_response_addr(u32 res)\n792: {\n793: \tunsigned int addr = res & 0xf;\n794: \n795: \tif (addr >= AZX_MAX_CODECS) {\n796: \t\tsnd_BUG();\n797: \t\taddr = 0;\n798: \t}\n799: \n800: \treturn addr;\n801: }\n802: \n803: /* send a command */\n804: static int azx_corb_send_cmd(struct hda_bus *bus, u32 val)\n805: {\n806: \tstruct azx *chip = bus->private_data;\n807: \tunsigned int addr = \tspin_unlock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n822: \n823: \treturn 0;\n824: }\n825: \n826: #define ICH6_RIRB_EX_UNSOL_EV\t(1<<4)\n827: \n828: /* retrieve RIRB entry - called from interrupt handler */\n829: static void azx_update_rirb(struct azx *chip)\n830: {\n831: \tunsigned int rp, wp;\n832: \tunsigned int addr;\n833: \tu32 res, res_ex;\n834: \n835: \twp = azx_readb(chip, RIRBWP);\n836: \tif (wp == \t\trp = chip->rirb.rp << 1; /* an RIRB entry is 8-bytes */\n845: \t\tres_ex = le32_to_cpu(chip->rirb.buf[rp + 1]);\n846: \t\tres = le32_to_cpu(chip->rirb.buf[rp]);\n847: \t\taddr = \t\t\tchip->rirb.res[addr] = res;\n852: \t\t\tsmp_wmb();\n853: \t\t\tchip->rirb.cmds[addr]--;\n854: \t\t} else\n855: \t\t\tsnd_printk(KERN_ERR SFX \"spurious response %#x:%#x, \"\n856: \t\t\t\t   \"last cmd=%#08x\\n\",\n857: \t\t\t\t   res, res_ex,\n858: \t\t\t\t   chip->last_cmd[addr]);\n859: \t}\n860: }\n861: \n862: /* receive a response */\n863: static unsigned int azx_rirb_get_response(struct hda_bus *bus,\n864: \t\t\t\t\t  unsigned int addr)\n865: {\n866: \tstruct azx *chip = bus->private_data;\n867: \tunsigned long timeout;\n868: \tunsigned long || do_poll) {\n876: \t\t\tspin_lock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n877: \t\t\tazx_update_rirb(chip);\n878: \t\t\tspin_unlock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n879: \t\t}\n880: \t\tif (!chip->rirb.cmds[addr]) {\n881: \t\t\t   \"polling the codec once: last cmd=0x%08x\\n\",\n901: \t\t\t   chip->last_cmd[addr]);\n902: \t\tdo_poll = 1;\n903: \t\tchip->poll_count++;\n904: \t\tgoto again;\n905: \t}\n906: \n907: \n908: \tif (!chip->polling_mode) {\n909: \t\tsnd_printk(KERN_WARNING SFX \"azx_get_response timeout, \"\n910: \t\t\t   \"switching to polling mode: last cmd=0x%08x\\n\",\n911: \t\t\t The command was\n964:  *       intended for the BIOS only, and may get confused with unsolicited\n965:  *       responses. */\n971: static int azx_single_wait_for_response(struct azx *chip, unsigned int addr)\n972: {\n973: \tint timeout = 50;\n974: \n975: \twhile (timeout--) {\n976: \t\t/* check IRV busy bit */\n977: = -1;\n988: \treturn -EIO;\n989: }\n990: \n991: /* send a command */\n992: static int azx_single_send_cmd(struct hda_bus *bus, u32 val)\n993: {\n994: \tstruct azx *chip = bus->private_data;\n995: azx_power_notify(struct hda_bus *bus, bool power_up);\n1062: #endif\n1063: \n1064: /* reset codec link */\n1065: static int azx_reset(struct azx *chip, int full_reset)\n1066: {\n1067: \tint interface\n1121:  */  \n1122: \n1123: /* enable interrupts */\n1124: static void azx_int_enable(struct azx *chip)\n1125: {\n1126: \t/* enable controller CIE and GIE */\n1127: \tazx_writel(chip, = 1;\n1230: }\n1231: \n1232: /*\n1233:  * initialize the PCI registers\n1234:  */\n1235: /* update bits in a PCI register byte */\n1236: static void update_pci_byte(struct pci_dev *pci, unsigned int & mask);\n1244: \tpci_write_config_byte(pci, reg, data);\n1245: }\n1246: \n1247: static void azx_init_pci(struct azx *chip)\n1248: {\n1249: \t/* Clear bits 0-2 of PCI register TCSEL (at offset updating\n2206:  * periods.  Returns non-zero if it's OK.\n2207:  *\n2208:  * Many HD-audio controllers appear pretty inaccurate about\n2209:  * the update-IRQ timing.  The IRQ is issued before actually the\n2210:  * data is processed.  So, we need to process it afterwords in a\n2211:  * workqueue.\n2212:  */\n2213: static int azx_position_ok(struct azx *chip, struct azx_dev *azx_dev)\n2214: {\n2215: \tu32 wallclk;\n2216: \tunsigned int pos;\n2217: \tint stream;\n2218: \n2219: \twallclk = azx_readl(chip, WALLCLK) - azx_dev->start_wallclk;\n2220: \tif (wallclk < (azx_dev->period_wallclk * 2) / 3)\n2221: \t\treturn -1;\t/* bogus (too early) interrupt */\n2222: \n2223: \tstream = azx_dev->substream->stream;\n2224: \tpos = azx_get_position(chip, azx_dev, true);\n2225: \n2226: \tif (WARN_ONCE(!azx_dev->period_bytes,\n2227: \t\t      \"hda-intel: zero azx_dev->period_bytes\"))\n2228: \t\treturn -1; /* this shouldn't happen! */\n2229: \tif (wallclk < (azx_dev->period_wallclk * 5) / 4 &&\n2230: \t    pos % azx_dev->period_bytes > azx_dev->period_bytes / 2)\n2231: \t\t/* NG - it's below the first next period boundary */\n2232: \t\treturn bdl_pos_adj[chip->dev_index] ? 0 : -1;\n2233: \tazx_dev->start_wallclk += wallclk;\n2234: \treturn 1; /* OK, it's fine */\n2235: }\n2236: \n2237: /*\n2238:  * The work for pending PCM period updates.\n2239:  */\n2240: static void azx_irq_pending_work(struct work_struct *work)\n2241: {\n2242: \tstruct azx *chip = container_of(work, struct azx, irq_pending_work);\n2243: \tint i, pending, ok;\n2244: \n2245: \tif (!chip->irq_pending_warned) {\n2246: \t\tprintk(KERN_WARNING\n2247: \t\t       \"hda-intel: IRQ timing workaround is activated \"\n2248: \t\t       \"for card #%d. This means the chip is not properly re-initialized after resume, which explains why communication with the codec times out.\n\n\nDuring suspend, `azx_suspend` stops the chip but never clears the `chip->initialized` flag. So when `azx_resume` calls `azx_init_chip(chip, 1)` with a full reset requested, the early return prevents the necessary re-initialization. In azx_init_chip:\n   - Calls azx_reset\n   - Clears and enables interrupts\n   - Initializes cmd I/O if not in single_cmd mode\n   - Programs position buffer\n   - Sets chip->initialized = 1\n\n3. The error messages show:\n   - Timeout getting response\n   - Switches to polling mode\n   - Disables MSI\n   - Switches to single_cmd mode\n\nThe issue might be that during suspend/resume, the polling_mode or single_cmd flags are not properly reset. Let me check if these flags are cleared during initialization.Looking at the azx_init_chip function, I don't see where polling_mode is reset to 0. This could be the issue! If after suspend, polling_mode is still set to 1 from a previous timeout, then when trying to get a response from the codec on resume, it might not work properly because it's already in polling mode This is an error recovery mode that's not the normal path. So if polling_mode is set to 1, all codec communication will go through the polling error recovery path instead of the normal interrupt-driven path!That's the issue! The codec communication is forced to use the error recovery/polling path even though the hardware is working normally after resume.So my analysis is correct. The fix is to reset polling_mode to 0 when full_reset is called in azx_init_chip.Actually, I should also consider if poll_count needs to be reset. \n\nIf poll_count isn't cleared and remains at 2 or higher, the condition at line 898 won't allow a single polling attempt on the next timeout—it'll bypass that check and immediately transition to polling mode. While this compounds the problem, resetting polling_mode itself is the critical fix since that's what forces all codec communication through the error recovery path after
